on_touch_move(self, touch):\n        if self.collide_point(*touch.pos):\n            self.line_points += [touch.x, touch.y]\n            return True\n        return super(SignaturePad, \"\"\"Login to Firebase Auth.\"\"\"\n    payload = {\n        'email': email,\n        'password': password,\n        'returnSecureToken': True\n    }\n    try:\n        resp = \"\"\"Save log entry to Firestore.\"\"\"\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {id_token}'}\n    doc = {\n        \"fields\": {k: {\"stringValue\": str(v)} for k, v in entry.items()}\n    }\n    # Use a unique documentId for each entry\n    safe_location = entry[\"location\"].replace(\" \", \"_\")\n    doc_id = f'{entry[\"date\"]}_{safe_location}_{user_id}'\n    url = f'{FIREBASE_DB_URL}?documentId={doc_id}'\n    resp = requests.patch(url, json=doc, headers=headers)\n    return resp.ok\n\ndef firebase_get_logs(id_token, user_id):\n    \"\"\"Get all logs for user from Firestore.\"\"\"\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {id_token}'}\n    url = f'{FIREBASE_DB_URL}?pageSize=100'\n    resp = requests.get(url, headers=headers)\n    logs = []\n    if \"\"\"Save log entry to Firestore.\"\"\"\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {id_token}'}\n    doc = {\n        \"fields\": {k: {\"stringValue\": str(v)} for k, v in entry.items()}\n    }\n    # validate_entry(data):\n    \"\"\"Validate logbook entry data.\"\"\"\n    try:\n        datetime.strptime(data['date'], '%Y-%m-%d')\n        assert data['location']\n        assert float(data['depth']) > 0\n        assert int(data['duration']) > 0\n        return True, ''\n    except Exception as e:\n        return False, f'Validation error: {e}'\n\ndef firebase_login(email, password):\n    \"\"\"Login to Firebase Auth.\"\"\"\n    payload = {\n        'email': email,\n        'password': password,\n        'returnSecureToken': True\n    }\n    try:\n        resp = requests.post(FIREBASE_AUTH_URL, json=payload)\n        data = resp.json()\n        if 'idToken' in data:\n            return True, data['idToken'], data['localId']\n        else:\n            return False, data.get('error', {}).get('message', 'Login failed'), None\n    except Exception as e:\n        return False, str(e), None\n\ndef firebase_register(email, password):\n    \"\"\"Register new user in Firebase Auth.\"\"\"\n    payload = {\n        'email': email,\n        'password': password,\n        'returnSecureToken': True\n    }\n    try:\n        resp = requests.post(FIREBASE_REGISTER_URL, json=payload)\n        data = resp.json()\n        if 'idToken' in data:\n            return True, data['idToken'], data['localId']\n        else:\n            return False, data.get('error', {}).get('message', 'Register failed'), None\n    except Exception as e:\n        return False, str(e), None\n\ndef firebase_save_log(id_token, user_id, entry):\n    \"\"\"Save log entry to Firestore.\"\"\"\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {id_token}'}\n    doc = {\n        \"fields\": {k: {\"stringValue\": str(v)} for k, v in entry.items()}\n    }\n    # Use a unique documentId for each entry\n    safe_location = entry[\"location\"].replace(\" \", \"_\")\n    doc_id = f'{entry[\"date\"]}_{safe_location}_{user_id}'\n    url = f'{FIREBASE_DB_URL}?documentId={doc_id}'\n    resp = requests.patch(url, json=doc, headers=headers)\n    return resp.ok\n\ndef firebase_get_logs(id_token, user_id):\n    \"\"\"Get all logs for user from Firestore.\"\"\"\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {id_token}'}\n    url = f'{FIREBASE_DB_URL}?pageSize=100'\n    resp = requests.get(url, headers=headers)\n    logs = []\n    if resp.ok:\n        data = resp.json()\n        for doc in data.get('documents', []):\n            fields = doc['fields']\n            log = {k: fields[k]['stringValue'] for k in fields}\n            if log.get('user_id') == user_id:\n                logs.append(log)\n    return logs\n\ndef firebase_upload_photo(id_token, file_path):\n    \"\"\"Upload photo to Firebase Storage.\"\"\"\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {id_token}'}\n    filename = os.path.basename(file_path)\n    with open(file_path, 'rb') as f:\n        files = {'file': f}\n        url = f'{FIREBASE_STORAGE_URL}/{filename}'\n        resp = requests.post(url, files=files, headers=headers)\n    if resp.ok:\n        return f'https://firebasestorage.googleapis.com/v0/b/{FIREBASE_STORAGE_BUCKET}/o/{filename}?alt=media'\n    else:\n        return ''\n\ndef ocr_image(file_path):\n    \"\"\"Extract text from image using OCR.\"\"\"\n    try:\n        img = PILImage.open(file_path)\n        text = pytesseract.image_to_string(img)\n        return text\n    except Exception as e:\n        return f'OCR error: {e}'\n\ndef export_csv(logs, filename='diver_logbook.csv'):\n    \"\"\"Export logs to CSV.\"\"\"\n    keys = ['date', 'location', 'depth', 'duration', 'notes']\n    with open(filename, 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=keys)\n        writer.writeheader()\n        for log in logs:\n            writer.writerow({k: log.get(k, '') for k in keys})\n {log.get('duration','')}min\")\n        textobject.textLine(f\"Notes: {log.get('notes','')}\")\n        textobject.textLine('-'*60)\n    c.drawText(textobject)\n    c.save()\n    return filename\n\n# ---- Kivy Screens ----\n\nclass LoginScreen(Screen):\n    status = StringProperty('')\n    email = ObjectProperty(None)\n    password = ObjectProperty(None)\n\n    def login(self):\n        email = \"\"\"Save log entry to Firestore.\"\"\"\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {id_token}'}\n    doc = {\n        \"fields\": {k: {\"stringValue\": str(v)} for k, v in entry.items()}\n    }\n    # from Firestore.\"\"\"\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {id_token}'}\n    url = f'{FIREBASE_DB_URL}?pageSize=100'\n    resp = requests.get(url, headers=headers)\n    logs = []\n    if requests.post(FIREBASE_REGISTER_URL, json=payload)\n        data = resp.json()\n        if 'idToken' in data:\n            return True, data['idToken'], data['localId']\n        else:\n            return False, data.get('error', {}).get('message', 'Register failed'), None\n    except Exception as e:\n        return False, str(e), None\n\ndef firebase_save_log(id_token, user_id, entry):\n    \"\"\"Save log entry to Firestore.\"\"\"\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {id_token}'}\n    doc = {\n        \"fields\": {k: {\"stringValue\": str(v)} for k, v in entry.items()}\n    }\n    # Use a unique documentId for each entry\n    safe_location = entry[\"location\"].replace(\" \", \"_\")\n    doc_id = f'{entry[\"date\"]}_{safe_location}_{user_id}'\n    url = f'{FIREBASE_DB_URL}?documentId={doc_id}'\n    resp = requests.patch(url, json=doc, headers=headers)\n    return resp.ok\n\ndef firebase_get_logs(id_token, user_id):\n    \"\"\"Get all logs for user from Firestore.\"\"\"\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {id_token}'}\n    url = f'{FIREBASE_DB_URL}?pageSize=100'\n    resp = requests.get(url, headers=headers)\n    logs = []\n    if resp.ok:\n        data = resp.json()\n        for doc in data.get('documents', []):\n            fields = doc['fields']\n            log = {k: fields[k]['stringValue'] for k in fields}\n            if log.get('user_id') == user_id:\n                logs.append(log)\n    return logs\n\ndef firebase_upload_photo(id_token, file_path):\n    \"\"\"Upload photo to Firebase Storage.\"\"\"\n    headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {id_token}'}\n    filename = os.path.basename(file_path)\n    # Firebase Storage simple upload via REST is limited; use multipart for demo\n    with open(file_path, 'rb') as f:\n        files = {'file': f}\n        url = f'{FIREBASE_STORAGE_URL}/{filename}'\n        resp = requests.post(url, files=files, headers=headers)\n    if resp.ok:\n        return f'https://firebasestorage.googleapis.com/v0/b/{FIREBASE_STORAGE_BUCKET}/o/{filename}?alt=media'\n    else:\n        return ''\n\ndef ocr_image(file_path):\n    \"\"\"Extract text from image using OCR.\"\"\"\n    try:\n        img = PILImage.open(file_path)\n        text = pytesseract.image_to_string(img)\n        return text\n    except Exception as e:\n        return f'OCR error: {e}'\n\ndef export_csv(logs, filename='diver_logbook.csv'):\n    \"\"\"Export logs to CSV.\"\"\"\n    keys = ['date', 'location', 'depth', 'duration', 'notes']\n    with open(filename, 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=keys)\n        writer.writeheader()\n        for log in logs:\n            writer.writerow({k: log.get(k, '') for k in keys})\n
